< Text>
Woodbridge is a wonderful country club. There are many activities to do including golfing, swimming, playing tennis, and more. The golf
course, and has won awards for it's incomparable flower gardening that attracts butteries and all around beauty. There are three nine hole courses, which allows for a different experience each time you play. To play the course or have access to the pool and tennis courts, you must have a membership though.</Text>

< text>
Woodbrige Country Club offers a variety of activities for their members. From a beautiful golf course to tennis courts to a delicious eat in restaurant, Woodbridge is a wonderful place to spend a day.
Woodbrige Country Club has one one the nicest golf courses in the central valley of California. The grounds are very well kept up and the plants are outstanding. The holes are decorated with beautiful flowers and trees lining the fairways. It is challenging for golfers of all levels, but is very fun to play. There are three different 9 hole courses on the grounds, each with its own characteristics. Overall the three courses make for an exciting and unique game.<//text>

Authenticity in an affordable price!!

I have tried many other mexican restaurants, some will look good outside but not inside when coming to food. But here it is opposite, in the beginning I didn‚Äôt even realized there existed a restaurant here. My friend recommended me this place. I was skeptical in the beginning about the food and quality. <gmapID>0x80c2b5f60e373937:0x68ee891a31c0a5a6< /gmapID><Pics>None<//Pics></record></dataset><record>

Mariela Chapina<//Name>
<gmapID>0x80c2b5f60e373937:0x68ee891a31c0a5a6<//gmapID>< review>
Little hole in the wall. My parent would bring me to this place since I was small, and I have done the same with my kids. The service is great, corn tortillas are freshly made, the food is also fresh and delicious. My favorite are the chorizo mulitas, and quesadillas de carne asada.  The facility is clean, and the parking is average. This is great place to try authentic Mexican food, which is usually hard to find, so I would totally recommend, but please note that it is a cash only place. However, if you forget to bring cash,  the little liquor store on the same shopping center has an ATM.< /review>

<Text>If you think storage should be convenient, or you want to get access to your stuff *Don't rent here*.

They will *not*  give any warning ,  and they will *not* discuss the matter with you, They will kick you out at the, first discovered event  (I say discovered because people break the rules all the time they just don't notice )

You will be given *2 DAYS* to find a new storage, rent a truck, and move (I had to move three truck loads), or they will repossess or trash can your stuff.

Do not stay late !!!!!!!!!
Do not smoke on permis (even in the parking lot , you have to go to the sidewalk)
Do not leave trash ( and I mean any trash !)
Do not  use the facility trash bin ( you have to pack it out in your car)
Do not store any unacceptable items (I.E. furniture ONLY! )
Do not park overnight ( They will absolutely tow you )

Any of these, will get you booted

So in my opinion it's better just to go down the street, there are plenty of places to store. (I liked Stor-All I had a pretty good experience with them.)

{'time': 1602265171176, 'text': 'Sorry you did not enjoy our prices, we provide an "a la carte" service, because some of our clients would rather avoid additional heat after a treatment or wash, and we share the sentiment since too much heat could dry out the effects of certain treatments. However, we always want it to be an option for clients who need to be dry in a hurry.\nIf you have the time during your next appointment, requesting to finish under the dryer, rather than requesting an active blow dry service is no extra charge and provides gentler heat circulation then active drying. Neither service provides a bone straightening effect, as the amount of heat that would be needed to achieve such a thing would unavoidably cause some level of damage and hair health is our primary concern.\n\nAs for consultations, we do provide in person consults only, as it is difficult to understand the hair needs over the phone. For hair, visual and even physicals confirmation, is always the best to avoid unnecessary precautions that could hinder rather then help and we would like to avoid giving advice or precautions that could lead to more harm then good.\n\nI hope you find this response satisfactory and helpful when booking your next service.'}<//resp>

<text>If I were on a deserted Island with only 1 restaurant to go to for the rest of my life, Mezzo would be the one. It is my dream girl of restaurants. Checks all my boxes and makes me feel both good and satisfied.

Our journey began years ago, when I was a young impressionable freshman in Berkeley. Every Wednesday I would get a chef salad after class and eat it for both my lunch and dinner. The portion was big enough that it could sustain even a growing boy like myself for two whole meals. The heartiness provided me comfort through countless disappointing test results, breakups, and failures. And the fact that it was primarily salad meant I didn't gain a single pound for it!

Bur if you're not into salad, their soup and sandwiches are also super yummy. Pretty much anything you get, you can try a sample beforehand. Make sure you take advantage of that if you have a hard time deciding. Regardless of how long the line is, the salaristas will make sure you get something you'll enjoy very much. 10/10. Highly recommended!

Fair warning: If you fall for this place, you may lose some friends. I have gotten more than a few horrified looks when I mention that my favorite restaurant in the whole wide world is a salad spot.<//text>< Pictures>

Mason Severe<//username>
< text>
A really cool, easily accessible, trendy spot in downtown Berkeley with excellent, organic foods!

I've lived in the Bay all my life but this was my first time actually coming to Mezzo. It's a lot of fun - it toes the line of casual but a little nicer too. Not to make a crude comparison, but it goes for a Chipotle vibe, just trendier and more original.

This place has a TON of seating - it was way more spacious than I could have expected with a lot of fun outdoor seating areas and open-air indoor seating too. Very communal type of seating arrangement and it seemed like everyone was having a really good time. Even when it's crowded it's not difficult to find somewhere to sit.

The food here is really quite phenomenal, you can tell it's all naturally sourced and fresh-made when you order. At a little above average price point for a casual meal, this is definitely a place I would stop at again in Berkeley if you have a group that just wants to get some really good salads and sandwiches.< /text>

Huge salads and sandwiches at reasonable prices.  With every gigantic salad,  you get a slice of bread and a piece of pineapple.  I always get the chef's salad with marinated tofu, hold the sprouts.

You can also get soup, half sandwich/salad and now they offer breakfast burritos.

This place is almost exactly like it's former self Intermezzo, but with a few more offerings and now it's credit cards only,  no cash.

The line moves fast, so don't be discouraged if there's a line out the door.</review>

< Review>
Warning: service here is super variable. If you order the same thing every time, you will undoubtedly get a different sandwich each time (in regards to quantity of ingredients, how the sandwich is put together). People enjoy the big portions here, but when someone skimps on your sandwich ingredients, it doesn't feel like a lot. Sometimes this inconsistency works in your favor, often times not. Overall though, the inconsistency is frustrating. I've ordered a BLTA to-go here and when I got home, I found no avocados... I mean... it's in the name! Generally, the BLTA is pretty good, lots of different components: sprouts, peppers, spicy mayo, crispy thick bacon, good tomatoes, and plenty of avocado slices (if they don't forget them or skimp). Bread is good, in particular I enjoyed the cheese jalapeno roll.

The soup is alright (Thai chicken and rice) but the chicken was a bit tough and chewy. Mint coffee is interesting as well, pretty good. Pastries are alright.

Overall, this place is okay. Service is fairly quick but the line can get horrifically long. At those times, it is definitely not worth the wait, in my opinion.< /Review>

<Resp>None</Resp><name>Grace Cadej< /name><Rating>5< /Rating>< UserId.>

< text>
I was a regular in the previous incarnation of Mezzo, back in the 90s, and couldn't get enough of their immense salads and hearty hummus sandwiches. I don't live in the area anymore, but whenever I visit I am drawn to Mezzo. The food is just like I remember it. A half sandwich and green salad could be skimpy in another restaurant, but here at Mezzo you're getting a generously filled sandwich -- you have to try their amazing honey wheat bread -- and not just a typical "side salad" but a full-fledged salad bowl with lettuce, cherry tomatoes, veggies, and croutons. So satisfying!

The old place was a little claustrophobic and known for unfriendly service, but now they have more space and a much nicer staff. They're doing something right! I hope they're around for years to come.<//text>

< Review>
It's now 9.50 for a veggie delight but otherwise the salad is the same size. Recently they've changed the poppuseed dressing for the worse - no longer a fan and can't find a suitable substitute. Vinaigrette is too sweet and the greek-yogurt-green-goddess didn't punch my happy ticket. The bread is still the same. Interestingly you can no longer pay cash. I wonder if it's intentional to keep Street people out. Atmosphere is super casual/relaxed. There's even a little couch area.<//Review>
